 The main objective of this course is to establish an excellent center for imparting high quality education and training the youth so that they can enter this profession with competence, skills and professional attitude
 dilli vishvavidhyalay ke kulapati yogesh tyaagi ne bataaya, ‘‘dilli vishvavidhyalay main prastaavit ‘dilli skool of jarnalism’ kaa mukhya uddeshy ucch gunvatttapurna shiksha pradaan karne ke liye ek utkrisht kendra sthapit karnaa or yuvaaon ko prashikshan dena he taaki ve kshamta, kaushal or peshevraana ravaiye ke saath is kshetra main pravesh karen
 '' unhone bataaya, ‘‘is paathyakram main reporting, editing or photography jaise kuch vishay vaise hi rahenge jo patrakarita ke moolbhoot aadhaar hai or chaatro ko padhaaye jate hai lekin isamen kuch nayaa bhi joda gaya he jo bilkul alag hoga
